BRA_setup_switch_parties_immune = {
	clear_array = BRA_switch_parties_immune
}

BRA_switch_parties = {
	set_temp_variable = { switch_party_id = tmp_from_party }
	set_temp_variable = { switch_party_id_2 = tmp_to_party }

	#display
	set_temp_variable = { party_id = switch_party_id }
	set_temp_variable = { party_id_2 = switch_party_id_2 }

	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { tmp_num_switch = 1 } }

		custom_effect_tooltip = BRA_senate_abandon
	}
	else = {
		custom_effect_tooltip = BRA_senate_abandon_plural
	}

	set_temp_variable = { tmp_num = tmp_num_switch }
	for_loop_effect = {
		start = 0
		end = tmp_num_switch
		value = j
		BRA_switch_parties_inner = yes
	}
}

BRA_switch_parties_one = {
	set_temp_variable = { switch_party_id_2 = tmp_to_party }
	set_temp_variable = { senator_id = tmp_senator }

	set_temp_variable = { switch_party_id = BRA_identities_parties^senator_id }

	set_variable = { BRA_identities_parties^senator_id = switch_party_id_2 }
	#display
	set_temp_variable = { party_id = switch_party_id }
	set_temp_variable = { party_id_2 = switch_party_id_2 }
	custom_effect_tooltip = BRA_senate_abandon_one

	clear_array = BRA_senator_parties_1
	clear_array = BRA_senator_parties_2
	clear_array = BRA_senator_parties_3
	for_each_loop = {
		array = BRA_senator_identities_1
		value = v
		add_to_array = { BRA_senator_parties_1 = BRA_identities_parties^v }
	}
	for_each_loop = {
		array = BRA_senator_identities_2
		value = v
		add_to_array = { BRA_senator_parties_2 = BRA_identities_parties^v }
	}
	for_each_loop = {
		array = BRA_senator_identities_3
		value = v
		add_to_array = { BRA_senator_parties_3 = BRA_identities_parties^v }
	}

	BRA_redraw_senate_diagram = yes
	BRA_senate_select_state = yes
}

BRA_switch_parties_inner = {
	set_temp_variable_to_random = s
	multiply_temp_variable = { s = 3 }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { s = 0.5 }
	round_temp_variable = s

	for_loop_effect = {
		start = 0
		end = 3
		value = v
		break = b

		set_temp_variable = { slot = s }
		add_to_temp_variable = { slot = v }
		modulo_temp_variable = { slot = 3 }

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { slot = 0 }
				is_in_array = { BRA_senator_parties_1 = switch_party_id }
			}
			for_each_loop = {
				array = BRA_senator_parties_1
				value = v_0
				index = i_0
				break = b_0
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { v_0 = switch_party_id }
						NOT = { is_in_array = { BRA_switch_parties_immune = BRA_senator_identities_1^i_0 } }
					}
					set_temp_variable = { senator_id = BRA_senator_identities_1^i_0 }
					set_temp_variable = { b_0 = 1 }
				}
			}
			set_temp_variable = { b = 1 } 
		}

		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { slot = 1 }
				is_in_array = { BRA_senator_parties_2 = switch_party_id }
			}
			for_each_loop = {
				array = BRA_senator_parties_2
				value = v_0
				index = i_0
				break = b_0
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { v_0 = switch_party_id }
						NOT = { is_in_array = { BRA_switch_parties_immune = BRA_senator_identities_2^i_0 } }
					}
					set_temp_variable = { senator_id = BRA_senator_identities_2^i_0 }
					set_temp_variable = { b_0 = 1 }
				}
			}
			set_temp_variable = { b = 1 } 
		}

		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { slot = 2 }
				is_in_array = { BRA_senator_parties_3 = switch_party_id }
			}
			for_each_loop = {
				array = BRA_senator_parties_3
				value = v_0
				index = i_0
				break = b_0
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { v_0 = switch_party_id }
						NOT = { is_in_array = { BRA_switch_parties_immune = BRA_senator_identities_3^i_0 } }
					}
					set_temp_variable = { senator_id = BRA_senator_identities_3^i_0 }
					set_temp_variable = { b_0 = 1 }
				}
			}
			set_temp_variable = { b = 1 } 
		}

		else = {
			set_temp_variable = { senator_id = 0 }
			set_temp_variable = { b = 1 } 
		}
	}

	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = {
				check_variable = { senator_id = 0 }
			}
		}
		set_variable = { BRA_identities_parties^senator_id = switch_party_id_2 }
	}

	BRA_redraw_senate_diagram = yes
	BRA_senate_select_state = yes
}

BRA_boost_ruling_party_candidates_nationwide_low = {
	if = {
		limit = { BRA_PTB_is_ruling_party = yes }
		BRA_boost_PTB_candidates_nationwide_low = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = { BRA_PSD_is_ruling_party = yes}
		BRA_boost_PSD_candidates_nationwide_low = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = { BRA_PTN_is_ruling_party = yes}
		BRA_boost_UDN_aligned_candidates_nationwide_low = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = { BRA_UDN_is_ruling_party = yes}
		BRA_boost_UDN_candidates_nationwide_low = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = { BRA_PSP_is_ruling_party = yes}
		BRA_boost_PSP_candidates_nationwide_low = yes
	}
}

	clear_array = BRA_modify_electoral_parties
	add_to_array = { BRA_modify_electoral_parties = 1 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_modify_electoral_parties = 11 }
}

BRA_setup_PSP_aligned = {
	clear_array = BRA_modify_electoral_parties
	add_to_array = { BRA_modify_electoral_parties = 8 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_modify_electoral_parties = 4 }
}

BRA_setup_low_amnt = {
	set_variable = { BRA_modify_amnt = 5 }
}
BRA_setup_med_amnt = {
	set_variable = { BRA_modify_amnt = 12.5 }
}
BRA_setup_high_amnt = {
	set_variable = { BRA_modify_amnt = 25 }
}

BRA_setup_neg_low_amnt = {
	set_variable = { BRA_modify_amnt = -5 }
}
BRA_setup_neg_med_amnt = {
	set_variable = { BRA_modify_amnt = -12.5 }
}
BRA_setup_neg_high_amnt = {
	set_variable = { BRA_modify_amnt = -25 }
}



BRA_modify_electoral_chances_nationwide = {
	clear_array = BRA_modify_electoral_states
	for_loop_effect = {
		start = 0
		end = 22
		value = i

		add_to_array = { BRA_modify_electoral_states = i }
	}
	BRA_modify_electoral_chances = yes
}

	add_to_array = { BRA_modify_electoral_states = 0 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_modify_electoral_states = 2 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_modify_electoral_states = 11 }

BRA_modify_electoral_chances_northeast = {
	clear_array = BRA_modify_electoral_states
	add_to_array = { BRA_modify_electoral_states = 1 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_modify_electoral_states = 3 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_modify_electoral_states = 4 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_modify_electoral_states = 8 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_modify_electoral_states = 12 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_modify_electoral_states = 14 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_modify_electoral_states = 15 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_modify_electoral_states = 17 }
	add_to_array = { BRA_modify_electoral_states = 21 }
	BRA_modify_electoral_chances = yes
}
BRA_modify_electoral_chances = {
	for_each_loop = {
		array = BRA_modify_electoral_states
		value = i
		index = k
		break = bo

		set_temp_variable = { lo = i }
		set_temp_variable = { hi = i }
		add_to_temp_variable = { hi = 1 }
		multiply_temp_variable = { lo = 8 }
		multiply_temp_variable = { hi = 8 }

		for_loop_effect = {
			start = lo
			end = hi
			value = j
			break = bi

			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { BRA_candidate_identities^j = 0 } }
				set_temp_variable = { break = 1 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { is_in_array = { array = BRA_modify_electoral_parties value = BRA_candidate_parties^j } }
				add_to_variable = { BRA_candidate_popularities^j = BRA_modify_amnt }
			}
		}
	}

	clear_array = BRA_modify_electoral_states
	clear_array = BRA_modify_electoral_parties
	BRA_update_leading_parties = yes
	BRA_senate_update_selected_state = yes
}

### OTHER SCRIPTED EFFECTS ###

BRA_boost_ruling_party_nationwide_low = {
	if = { # UDN
		limit = {
			BRA_UDN_is_ruling_party = yes
		}
		BRA_boost_UDN_candidates_nationwide_low = yes
	}
	if = { # PTB
		limit = {
			BRA_PTB_is_ruling_party = yes
		}
		BRA_boost_PTB_candidates_nationwide_low = yes
	}
	if = { # PSD
		limit = {
			BRA_PSD_is_ruling_party = yes
		}
		BRA_boost_PSD_candidates_nationwide_low = yes
	}
	if = { # PSP
		limit = {
			BRA_PSP_is_ruling_party = yes
		}
		BRA_boost_PSP_candidates_nationwide_low = yes
	}
}

	if = { # UDN
		limit = {
			BRA_UDN_is_ruling_party = yes
		}
		BRA_boost_UDN_candidates_nationwide_med = yes
	}
	if = { # PTB
		limit = {
			BRA_PTB_is_ruling_party= yes
		}
		BRA_boost_PTB_candidates_nationwide_med = yes
	}
	if = { # PSD
		limit = {
			BRA_PSD_is_ruling_party = yes
		}
		BRA_boost_PSD_candidates_nationwide_med = yes
	}
	if = { # PSP
		limit = {
			BRA_PSP_is_ruling_party = yes

	}

			BRA_PTB_is_ruling_party= yes
		}
		BRA_harm_PTB_candidates_nationwide_high = yes
	}
	if = { # PSD
		limit = {
			BRA_PSD_is_ruling_party = yes
		}
		BRA_harm_PSD_candidates_nationwide_high = yes
	}
	if = { # PSP
		limit = {
			BRA_PSP_is_ruling_party = yes
		}
		BRA_harm_PSP_candidates_nationwide_high = yes
	}
}
